  ```dart
  class MainNavigation extends StatefulWidget {
    const MainNavigation({super.key});

    @override
    State<MainNavigation> createState() => _MainNavigationState();
  }

  class _MainNavigationState extends State<MainNavigation> {
    int _currentIndex = 0;

    // Список всех экранов приложения
    final List<Widget> _screens = [
      const HomeScreen(),
      const BlogScreen(),
      const MapScreen(),
      const StoreScreen(),
      const ProfileScreen(),
    ];

    @override
    Widget build(BuildContext context) {
      return ValueListenableBuilder<String?>(
        valueListenable: ApiService.tokenNotifier,
        builder: (context, token, child) {
          if (token == null) {
            return AuthScreen(
              onLoginSuccess: () {
                setState(() {
                  _currentIndex = 0;
                });
              },
            );
          }

          return ValueListenableBuilder<String>(
            valueListenable: AppState().currentLanguage,
            builder: (context, lang, child) {
              final state = AppState();
              return Scaffold(
                body: IndexedStack(
                  index: _currentIndex,
                  children: _screens,
                ),
                bottomNavigationBar: BottomNavigationBar(
                  currentIndex: _currentIndex,
                  onTap: (index) => setState(() => _currentIndex = index),
                  items: [
                    BottomNavigationBarItem(icon: const Icon(Icons.school), label: state.translate('nav_courses')),
                    BottomNavigationBarItem(icon: const Icon(Icons.article), label: state.translate('nav_news')),
                    BottomNavigationBarItem(icon: const Icon(Icons.map), label: state.translate('nav_map')),
                    BottomNavigationBarItem(icon: const Icon(Icons.shopping_cart), label: state.translate('nav_shop')),
                    BottomNavigationBarItem(icon: const Icon(Icons.person), label: state.translate('nav_profile')),
                  ],
                ),
              );
            },
          );
        },
      );
    }
  }
  ```

- Added `register(String name, String email, String password)` to connect to the backend registration API.

- Added `tokenNotifier` (a `ValueNotifier\u003cString?\u003e` wrapper for the authentication token). Whenever a session is saved or cleared, the notifier triggers rebuilds on active listeners in the app.

### 3. Comprehensive Authentication Screen (`mobile/lib/auth_screen.dart`)
- Created a new UI styled in the dark neon-blue and glassmorphic palette.
- Features **Вход** (Login) and **Регистрация** (Register) tabs.

  - Uses `Timer` to transition to the main page after **3.5 seconds**.
- **Root App Lock:**
  - Updated `MainNavigation` to listen to `ApiService.tokenNotifier`.
  - If the token is null, it renders the `AuthScreen` directly, completely hiding the main navigation tabs and bottom navigation bar.
  - Logging out immediately sets the token to null, instantly locking the app and redirecting the user to `AuthScreen`.

- Simplified the class by removing the redundant local login view and forms.
- Re-routed the "Выйти" (Logout) button to clear the global `ApiService` session, triggering the global lock.

## Proposed Changes

### Backend

We will introduce a temporary registration store to verify users via email before creating them in the database.

#### [MODIFY] [package.json](file:///d:/skycheck/backend/package.json)
- Add `nodemailer` dependency to support email sending.

#### [MODIFY] [server.js](file:///d:/skycheck/backend/server.js)
- Import `nodemailer`.
- Set up an email transporter using environment variables (`SMTP_HOST`, `SMTP_PORT`, `SMTP_USER`, `SMTP_PASS`) with a fallback logger to print the email to the console.
- Add an in-memory `pendingRegistrations` store (`Map`) to save `{ email: { name, password, code, expires } }`.
- Modify `POST /auth/register` to:
  - Generate a random 6-digit code.
  - Store user info and code in `pendingRegistrations`.
  - Send the verification email to the user (or log to console).
  - Return a status `{ success: true, message: 'VERIFICATION_REQUIRED' }`.
- Add a new endpoint `POST /auth/verify-code` which:
  - Receives `email` and `code`.
  - Validates the code.
  - Hash the password, creates the user in Prisma database, deletes code from the store.
  - Signs a JWT token and returns user details.

---

We will update theme management, build the email confirmation UI, and design the animated splash screen.

- Import `package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart`.
- Add an `init()` method to load `isDarkMode` and `currentLanguage` from disk.
- Update `toggleTheme()` and `setLanguage()` to write updates to `SharedPreferences` asynchronously.

#### [MODIFY] [main.dart](file:///d:/skycheck/mobile/lib/main.dart)
- Update `main()` to initialize `AppState()` after `ApiService.init()`.
- **Upgraded Splash Screen:**

    - **Stage 1 (0-1.5s):** Smooth elastic scale-up and rotation of the flight icon.

    - **Stage 3 (1.5-3.0s):** Fade-in and vertical slide-up of "SkyCheck УЗБЕКИСТАН" logo text.

### 👤 Ассистент:
**Examining App Initialization**

I'm now investigating the `AppState` initialization, specifically within the `main.dart` file. I've noted the sequence: `WidgetsFlutterBinding.ensureInitialized()`, followed by `ApiService.init()`, before the app runs. I see a necessity to load preferences before `runApp()` to ensure their availability during the app's startup phase.


**Implementing App State Initialization**

I've made significant progress by implementing the `init()` method within `AppState` to load stored values from `SharedPreferences`, specifically for dark mode and current language. The changes include adding `import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';`, and modifying `main()` to `await AppState().init();` ensuring the theme and language are loaded before the app runs. The `toggleTheme()` and `setLanguage()` methods were modified to save these values.


**Refining Splash Screen Animation**

I've achieved synchronous theme loading, eliminating startup flicker! Now, I'm focusing on a premium splash screen. I'm designing distinct light and dark mode animations: a dark, cyberpunk neon space aesthetic versus a light, clean modern look. I'm exploring advanced animation techniques, potentially using multi-stage animation controllers, to achieve a smooth and polished experience.


**Designing Splash Screen Elements**

I'm now diving into the specifics of crafting the splash screen visuals. I'm prioritizing a glowing radial gradient background with animated inner and outer rings, evocative of radar and motion. The "Flight" icon will scale with a bounce effect and subtle floating. I'm exploring fading text effects for "SkyCheck" and a sliding glow for the subtitle "УЗБЕКИСТАН". I intend to create a Stateful Widget for a truly interactive feel. I'm sketching out a dark navy gradient for dark mode.


**Constructing Splash Screen Animations**

I'm now deep in the animation mechanics. I've broken down the 3.5-second duration into intervals for precise control. I'm leveraging `CurvedAnimation` with an `AnimationController` for complex, staged effects. Specifically, I'm setting up separate `_logoScale`, `_logoRotate`, and `_pulseAnimation` controllers using different intervals, using elasticOut and easeOutBack for a dynamic feel. I'm focusing on making the pulse a visual component.

**Considering Data Structures**

I've decided against altering the database schema for verification codes, opting instead for an in-memory `Map` within `server.js` to store pending registrations and their associated codes. This approach is cleaner, safer, and avoids any potential production database migration issues. The `pendingRegistrations` Map is looking like the best option.

'{"AllowMultiple":false,"Description":"Update registration and add code verification in server.js","EndLine":225,"Instruction":"Replace registration endpoint and add verify-code endpoint","ReplacementContent":"app.post('/auth/register', async (req, res) =\u003e {
  try {
    const { email, password, name } = req.body;
    if (!email || !password || !name) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Все поля обязательны' });
    if (password.length \u003c 6) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Пароль должен быть не менее 6 символов' });
    if (!email.includes('@')) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Неверный формат Email' });

    const existingUser = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { email } });
    if (existingUser) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Email уже используется' });

    // Generate random 6-digit code
    const code = Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000).toString();
    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);

    // Save to pending store
    pendingRegistrations.set(email.toLowerCase(), {
      name,
      email,
      password: hashedPassword,
      code,
      expires: Date.now() + 10 * 60 * 1000 // 10 minutes
    });

    // Send email
    await sendVerificationEmail(email, code);

    res.json({
      success: true,
      message: 'VERIFICATION_REQUIRED',
      email: email
    });
  } catch (e) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Ошибка сервера при регистрации' });
  }
});

app.post('/auth/verify-code', async (req, res) =\u003e {
  try {
    const { email, code } = req.body;
    if (!email || !code) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Email и код обязательны' });

    const pending = pendingRegistrations.get(email.toLowerCase());
    if (!pending) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Регистрационная сессия не найдена или истекла' });
    }

    if (Date.now() \u003e pending.expires) {
      pendingRegistrations.delete(email.toLowerCase());
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Срок действия кода подтверждения истек' });
    }

    if (pending.code !== code) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Неверный код подтверждения' });
    }

    // Check again to be absolutely sure the email was not registered in the meantime
    const existingUser = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { email: pending.email } });
    if (existingUser) {
      pendingRegistrations.delete(email.toLowerCase());
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Email уже зарегистрирован' });
    }

    // Create user
    const user = await prisma.user.create({
      data: {
        email: pending.email,
        password: pending.password,
        name: pending.name,
        role: 'user',
      },
    });

    // Remove from pending
    pendingRegistrations.delete(email.toLowerCase());

    const token = jwt.sign({ id: user.id, email: user.email, role: user.role }, JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn: '7d' });
    res.json({
      token,
      user: {
        id: user.id,
        name: user.name,
        email: user.email,
        role: user.role,
        exp: user.exp,
        level: user.level,
        achievements: []
      }
    });
  } catch (e) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Ошибка сервера при проверке кода' });
  }

### 👤 Ассистент:
Changes Made

### 1. Theme and Language Persistence (`mobile/lib/app_state.dart`)
- Integrated `package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart` into `AppState`.
- Implemented an `init()` method that loads stored values synchronously before the application UI renders.
- Updated `toggleTheme()` and `setLanguage()` to write modifications directly to local storage to ensure persistent user choices.

### 2. Startup Optimization (`mobile/lib/main.dart`)
- Updated the entry point `main()` to await `AppState().init()` before running `runApp()`. This eliminates startup flickers and ensures the app matches the persisted theme immediately.

### 3. Upgraded Premium Splash Screen (`mobile/lib/main.dart`)
- **Dual-Theme Design:**
  - **Dark Mode:** Deep space radial gradient, glowing neon cyan/blue elements, cybernetic ring overlays, and modern Outfit typography.
  - **Light Mode:** Bright ice-blue/white radial gradient, elegant royal blue accents, clean white cards with soft drop shadows, and dark typography.
- **Dynamic Animation Engine:**
  - **Stage 1 (Intro):** Bouncy elastic scale and rotational entry of the flight icon.
  - **Stage 2 (Pulsing Radar):** Multiple concentric circles expanding and fading outwards dynamically, simulating sonar scans.
  - **Stage 3 (Hovering Flight):** Continuous vertical floating animation mimicking a drone hovering.
  - **Stage 4 (Typography):** Opacity fade-in paired with a letter-spacing compression transition for the logo text.
  - Smooth 500ms fade transition into the main app container.

### 4. Code Verification UI (`mobile/lib/auth_screen.dart` \u0026 `mobile/lib/api_service.dart`)
- Added `verifyCode` to the mobile networking client to send registration confirmation details.
- Integrated a **Подтверждение почты** (Email Verification) card that transitions dynamically upon a successful registration step.
- Displays the target email address and offers a numerical input field to submit the 6-digit verification code.
- Includes a TextButton to allow returning to the registration form and editing details.

### 5. Email Verification Backend (`backend/server.js` \u0026 `backend/package.json`)
- Added `nodemailer` to dependencies to handle real email delivery.
- Set up SMTP transport with clean configuration parameters and a robust console logging fallback for local testing.
- Introduced an in-memory `pendingRegistrations` session map to hold temporary pilot profiles securely before DB inclusion.
- Updated `POST /auth/register` to check for duplicates, generate code, and send verification messages.
- Created `POST /auth/verify-code` to confirm the pin, write the user to the Postgres instance, and issue JWT session tokens.

Вот подробный отчет по проделанной работе:

### 1. Сохранение и восстановление темы (Dark/Light Mode)
* **Проблема:** Выбранная светлая или темная тема сбрасывалась при перезапуске приложения.
* **Решение:** 
  * Внедрил интеграцию с `SharedPreferences` в синглтон [AppState](file:///d:/skycheck/mobile/lib/app_state.dart) для сохранения ключей темы (`isDarkMode`) и языка (`currentLanguage`).
  * Метод `AppState().init()` теперь вызывается и ожидается (`await`) непосредственно в функции `main()` в файле [main.dart](file:///d:/skycheck/mobile/lib/main.dart) перед запуском `runApp()`. Это полностью устраняет эффект мерцания (flicker) и гарантирует, что приложение сразу же открывается в нужной цветовой схеме.

### 2. Премиальная анимация при запуске (Splash Screen) под Светлую и Темную темы
* **Проблема:** Старая анимация выглядела простой, не адаптировалась под тему и длилась недолго.
* **Решение:** Полностью переработал [SplashScreen](file:///d:/skycheck/mobile/lib/main.dart#L76-L209) с разделением на две стилистики:
  * **Темная версия:** Радиальный градиент космического синего цвета, неоново-циановые светящиеся элементы, кибернетические круги с размытыми тенями и контрастный белый шрифт.
  * **Светлая версия:** Светло-голубой ледяной градиент, аккуратная белая плашка с мягкой размытой тенью, королевский синий значок самолета/дрона и глубокий темно-серый заголовок.
  * **Анимационный движок:** Объединил три независимых контроллера (`TickerProviderStateMixin`) для создания невероятно плавного эффекта:
    1. *Появление:* Самолет упруго увеличивается (`elasticOut`) и плавно прокручивается на место (`easeOutBack`).
    2. *Радар (сигнал дрона):* От значка бесконечно расходятся и затухают два концентрических неоновых кольца.
    3. *Левитация (hover):* Значок непрерывно покачивается вверх-вниз, имитируя зависший в воздухе дрон.
    4. *Текст:* Заголовок

0**Analyzing the structure now**

**Investigating a logic bug**

I've discovered a critical logic flaw. Lessons without associated questions lack a completion trigger in the UI, rendering them unfinishable. I traced this behavior to a design oversight where completion relies on a question-answer validation via a backend endpoint (`/courses/steps/:stepId/complete`). The seed data currently uses questions for every step. The implications are significant, as non-question-based lessons cannot be marked as "completed" by design, without a backend change.


**Defining the Data Structures**

**Evaluating the Backend Flow**

I'm now deep in the process of auditing the backend quiz validation logic. My current focus is on the crucial issue of securely handling quiz answers. The system is designed to match the submitted option text against the correct answer text stored by the backend, after shuffling the question and options on the backend. This safeguards the answer's security, and requires a modification to the backend data retrieval. I'm checking existing code now to remove `answer` data.


**Designing a Secure Submission**

I am now designing a robust and secure quiz submission flow. When the client submits answers via `POST /courses/steps/:stepId/submit` (or `/complete`), it will send option texts or matching question-answer pairs. The backend will fetch the original questions, find the correct option text, and verify matches. This stateless approach ensures security and works regardless of shuffling. The validation design is: stateless, highly secure, and works even if shuffled!


**Refining the Quiz Submission**

I'm now refining the quiz submission logic. I realized, the questions require a "topic" field to be fully functional! I'm moving toward a more user-friendly error response after a failed quiz attempt, highlighting only the failed topic areas and the correct answers. I'm also now considering adding a `topic` field to the `questions` property on the `CourseStep` to allow for such reporting. The plan is to enhance the user experience.


**Implementing Topic Identification**

I'm now detailing topic retrieval for quiz feedback. My design now prioritizes a question's `topic` field, returning that for failed answers. If no `topic` is present on a question, I will default to the lesson step's title for topic identification. This offers flexibility.

**Defining the Attempt Cooldown**

I am now implementing the cooldown logic for quiz attempts. I am defining a 30-minute cooldown after the second failed attempt, and a 24-hour cooldown after the fourth. With a maximum of 5 attempts before admin intervention, I'm now tracing the unsuccessful attempts counter. I'm verifying attempt counts to trigger the appropriate cooldown, to provide the exact requested user requirements.


**Tracking the course progress**

I am now focusing on implementing the course progression logic, which will be stored in `UserLessonProgress`. I'll track statuses: `not_started`, `in_progress`, and `completed`. Steps unlock sequentially, and a "final exam" step can now be added. I'm adding a new step at the end of each course: "Финальный экзамен". I'll be adding questions to this step.


**Implementing Video Control**

I'm now implementing the video control feature and the course progress tracking. I'm focusing on the `UserLessonProgress` model, storing `lesson_started_at`, and `is_timer_completed`. I'm determining the logic for the "Next Step" button, only allowing progress once video duration (or estimated read time) has passed. I am managing the interplay between backend and frontend states, ensuring timer persistence. I am now taking into consideration the implementation of progress tracking of a text-based lesson.


**Unifying Lesson Progress**

I'm now detailing the implementation for unifying text and video lesson progress tracking. I'll record `lesson_started_at` for text lessons when opened and calculate `estimated_read_time` based on text length. Completion hinges on time spent, `estimated_read_time`, and scroll completion (`scroll_completed`), unifying both lesson types. I am checking the logic for `lesson_started_at`.

We will implement a rigorous progression checking system, secure course content from unauthorized screen captures, and build a comprehensive administrative dashboard for user and course management.

---

## User Review Required

\u003e [!IMPORTANT]
\u003e **Database Migrations:** We will add 5 new models (`UserBlock`, `AdminAction`, `UserLessonProgress`, `UserCourseBlock`, `ScreenshotViolation`) and modify existing `User`, `Course`, `CourseStep`, and `CourseCompletion` models. This requires running `npx prisma migrate dev`.
\u003e **External Screen Protection:** On Android, we will use `flutter_windowmanager` to enforce system-level `FLAG_SECURE`. On iOS, we will natively intercept screenshots and screen recordings in the view tree, displaying a warning screen and sending a logging request to the backend.

\u003e [!IMPORTANT]
\u003e 1. **Final Exam Definition:** We propose adding a new step `isFinalExam: true` at the end of each course in `seed_advanced_courses.js` containing 5 comprehensive questions, separate from intermediate step quizzes. Please confirm if this matches your requirement.

### Backend

#### [MODIFY] [server.js](file:///d:/skycheck/backend/server.js)
- **Quiz Shuffling \u0026 Protection:**
  - Add `GET /courses/steps/:stepId/quiz` to return questions with shuffled questions and option lists, **completely omitting the `answer` index** to prevent client-side inspection.
  - Add `POST /courses/steps/:stepId/quiz-submit` to receive selected answer text, evaluate against DB answers, enforce 80% passing grade (95% for exams), track attempts (max 5), and calculate cooldown (30 min after 2nd fail, 24 hr after 4th fail).
- **Time Controls:**
  - Add `POST /courses/steps/:stepId/start` to register `lessonStartedAt` and set status to `in_progress`.
  - Modify step completion (`/complete`) to require `current_time \u003e= lessonStartedAt + duration` (video duration or calculated text estimated read time) and `scrollCompleted === true` (for text).
- **Required Progression Sequence:**
  - Enforce that a step cannot be completed or started if the previous step is not `completed`.
  - Enforce that a final exam step cannot be started if all previous steps in the module are not `completed`.
- **Certificate Verification:**
  - Add `GET /verify-certificate/:uuid` to serve a public, beautiful HTML verification page confirming validity, name, course, and score.
- **Violation Logging:**
  - Add `POST /courses/steps/:stepId/violation` to log screenshots. Lock user-course access if count reaches 5.
- **Admin Dashboard API Extension:**
  - Extend `/admin/users` to return active users list with status, courses started, progress %, and blocked status.
  - Add `GET /admin/users/:id/detail` to return user's module progression tree, quiz scores, attempts, and screenshot logs.
  - Add `POST /admin/users/:id/block` and `POST /admin/users/:id/unblock` to manage access.
  - Add `POST /admin/users/:id/reset-quiz` and `POST /admin/users/:id/reset-timer` to clear constraints.

  - Add `FLAG_SECURE` in `initState` and clear in `dispose` to block Android captures.

  - Integrate scroll controller listener in `StepDetailScreen` to set `scrollCompleted = true` when bottom is reached.
  - Read `estimated_read_time` and show countdown timer overlay ("Следующий шаг доступен через XX:XX") with a disabled button.

```
POST /courses/steps/:stepId/start
```

```javascript
app.post('/courses/steps/:stepId/start', authMiddleware, async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const stepId = parseInt(req.params.stepId);
        const { userId } = req.user;

        // Check if user is blocked for this course
        const isBlocked = await UserCourseBlock.findOne({ userId, courseId });
        if (isBlocked) {
            return res.status(403).json({ error: "Доступ к курсу временно заблокирован на 24 часа из-за нарушений политики безопасности (скриншоты/запись экрана)." });
        }

        // Validate sequence
        const currentStep = await Step.findByPk(stepId);
        if (!currentStep) {
            return res.status(404).json({ error: "Урок не найден" });
        }
        const courseId = currentStep.courseId;
        const previousStep = await Step.findOne({
            where: { courseId, stepOrder: { [Op.lt]: currentStep.stepOrder } },
            order: [['stepOrder', 'DESC']]
        });

        // If there is a previous step and its status is not completed, block
        if (previousStep) {
            const previousProgress = await UserLessonProgress.findOne({ where: { userId, stepId: previousStep.id } });
            if (!previousProgress || previousProgress.status !== 'completed') {
                return res.status(403).json({ error: "Нельзя начать следующий урок, не завершив предыдущий." });
            }
        }

        // Get lesson progress
        let progress = await UserLessonProgress.findOne({ where: { userId, stepId } });

        // If progress does not exist, create it. Otherwise, return the existing lessonStartedAt value.
        if (!progress) {
            progress = await UserLessonProgress.create({
                userId,
                stepId,
                status: 'in_progress',
                lessonStartedAt: new Date(),
            });
        } else if (progress.status === 'completed') {
            return res.status(403).json({ error: "Этот урок уже пройден." });
        }
        return res.json({
            status: progress.status,
            lessonStartedAt: progress.lessonStartedAt,
            // You might want to return estimatedTime here
        });

    } catch (error) {
        console.error(error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal Server Error" });
    }
});
```
```

```

Video steps will require checks for elapsed time versus the video duration. Quiz completion is now handled through `/quiz-submit` and includes score calculation.

The backend will now return the violation count, and after 5 violations, I'll block the user's access to the course and return the block status and time.

app.get('/admin/users-dashboard', adminMiddleware, async (req, res) =\u003e {
  try {
    const { search, sort, order } = req.query; // sort: "startDate" | "progress" | "lastActivity"; order: "asc" | "desc"
    
    // Fetch all courses to know step counts
    const courses = await prisma.course.findMany({
      include: { steps: true }
    });
    const courseStepCounts = {};
    courses.forEach(c =\u003e {
      courseStepCounts[c.id] = c.steps.length;
    });

    // Fetch all users with their lesson progress
    const users = await prisma.user.findMany({
      include: {
        lessonProgress: {
          include: { step: true }
        }
      }
    });

    const dashboardData = [];

    for (const user of users) {
      // Group progress by courseId
      const courseGroups = {};
      user.lessonProgress.forEach(lp =\u003e {
        const cId = lp.step.courseId;
        if (!courseGroups[cId]) courseGroups[cId] = [];
        courseGroups[cId].push(lp);
      });

      for (const cId in courseGroups) {
        const progressList = courseGroups[cId];
        const courseId = parseInt(cId);
        const course = courses.find(c =\u003e c.id === courseId);
        if (!course) continue;

        const completedCount = progressList.filter(lp =\u003e lp.status === 'completed').length;
        const totalSteps = courseStepCounts[courseId] || 1;
        const progressPercent = Math.round((completedCount / totalSteps) * 100);

        const startTimes = progressList.map(lp =\u003e lp.lessonStartedAt).filter(Boolean);
        const updateTimes = progressList.map(lp =\u003e lp.updatedAt).filter(Boolean);

        const startDate = startTimes.length \u003e 0 ? new Date(Math.min(...startTimes.map(d =\u003e d.getTime()))) : new Date();
        const lastActivity = updateTimes.length \u003e 0 ? new Date(Math.max(...updateTimes.map(d =\u003e d.getTime()))) : new Date();

        dashboardData.push({
          userId: user.id,
          name: user.name,
          email: user.email,
          isBlocked: user.isBlocked,
          courseId,
          courseTitle: course.title,
          startDate,
          lastActivity,
          progressPercent
        });
      }
    }

    // Filter by search
    let filtered = dashboardData;
    if (search) {
      const s = search.toLowerCase();
      filtered = filtered.filter(row =\u003e row.name.toLowerCase().includes(s) || row.email.toLowerCase().includes(s));
    }

    // Sort
    if (sort) {
      const ord = order === 'desc' ? -1 : 1;
      filtered.sort((a, b) =\u003e {
        if (sort === 'startDate') {
          return (a.startDate.getTime() - b.startDate.getTime()) * ord;
        } else if (sort === 'progress') {
          return (a.progressPercent - b.progressPercent) * ord;
        } else if (sort === 'lastActivity') {
          return (a.lastActivity.getTime() - b.lastActivity.getTime()) * ord;
        }
        return 0;
      });
    } else {
      // Default sort by last activity desc
      filtered.sort((a, b) =\u003e b.lastActivity.getTime() - a.lastActivity.getTime());
    }

    res.json(filtered);
  } catch (e) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
  }

app.get('/admin/users/:id/detail', adminMiddleware, async (req, res) =\u003e {
  try {
    const userId = parseInt(req.params.id);
    const user = await prisma.user.findUnique({
      where: { id: userId },
      select: { id: true, name: true, email: true, isBlocked: true, blockedAt: true, blockedBy: true, blockReason: true }
    });
    if (!user) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Пользователь не найден' });

    // Fetch all courses and steps
    const courses = await prisma.course.findMany({
      include: {
        steps: {
          orderBy: { order: 'asc' }
        }
      },
      orderBy: { id: 'asc' }
    });

    // Fetch user progress for this user
    const progresses = await prisma.userLessonProgress.findMany({
      where: { userId },
      include: { step: true }
    });
    const progressMap = new Map(progresses.map(p =\u003e [p.stepId, p]));

    // Build courses details
    const courseDetails = courses.map(course =\u003e {
      let completedCount = 0;
      const steps = course.steps.map(step =\u003e {
        const prog = progressMap.get(step.id);
        const status = prog ? prog.status : 'not_started';
        if (status === 'completed') completedCount++;

        return {
          id: step.id,
          title: step.title,
          type: step.type,
          isFinalExam: step.isFinalExam,
          status,
          lessonStartedAt: prog ? prog.lessonStartedAt : null,
          timeSpentSeconds: prog ? prog.timeSpentSeconds : 0,
          isTimerCompleted: prog ? prog.isTimerCompleted : false,
          quizAttempts: prog ? prog.quizAttempts : 0,
          cooldownUntil: prog ? prog.cooldownUntil : null,
          updatedAt: prog ? prog.updatedAt : null
        };
      });

      const totalSteps = course.steps.length || 1;
      const progressPercent = Math.round((completedCount / totalSteps) * 100);

      return {
        courseId: course.id,
        courseTitle: course.title,
        progressPercent,
        steps
      };
    });

    // Fetch timeline of user activity:
    const violations = await prisma.screenshotViolation.findMany({
      where: { userId },
      include: { step: true },
      orderBy: { timestamp: 'desc' }
    });

    const timeline = [];
    progresses.forEach(p =\u003e {
      timeline.push({
        type: 'progress_update',
        timestamp: p.updatedAt,
        message: `Урок "${p.step.title}": статус изменен на "${p.status}"`
      });
      if (p.lessonStartedAt) {
        timeline.push({
          type: 'lesson_started',
          timestamp: p.lessonStartedAt,
          message: `Начато изучение урока "${p.step.title}"`
        });
      }
    });

    violations.forEach(v =\u003e {
      timeline.push({
        type: 'violation',
        timestamp: v.timestamp,
        message: `Нарушение политики скриншотов на уроке "${v.step.title}"`
      });
    });

    // Sort timeline desc by timestamp
    timeline.sort((a, b) =\u003e new Date(b.timestamp) - new Date(a.timestamp));

    // Admin notifications flags
    const exhaustedAttempts = progresses.some(p =\u003e p.quizAttempts \u003e= 5);
    
    // Check if blocked by screenshots in UserCourseBlock
    const courseBlock = await prisma.userCourseBlock.findFirst({
      where: { userId, blockedUntil: { gt: new Date() } }
    });
    const screenshotBlocked = !!courseBlock;

    // Check inactivity: last progress update older than 7 days, and at least one course is started but not 100% complete
    let inactiveAlert = false;
    if (progresses.length \u003e 0) {
      const lastUpdate = new Date(Math.max(...progresses.map(p =\u003e p.updatedAt.getTime())));
      const daysInactive = (Date.now() - lastUpdate.getTime()) / 1000 / 60 / 60 / 24;
      
      const incompleteCourseExists = courseDetails.some(cd =\u003e cd.progressPercent \u003e 0 \u0026\u0026 cd.progressPercent \u003c 100);
      if (daysInactive \u003e 7 \u0026\u0026 incompleteCourseExists) {
        inactiveAlert = true;
      }
    }

    res.json({
      user,
      courses: courseDetails,
      timeline: timeline.slice(0, 30), // limit to last 30 events
      notifications: {
        exhaustedAttempts,
        screenshotBlocked,
        inactiveAlert
      }
    });
  } catch (e) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
  }
});

app.post('/admin/users/:id/block', adminMiddleware, async (req, res) =\u003e {
  try {
    const userId = parseInt(req.params.id);
    const { reason } = req.body;

    const user = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
    if (!user) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Пользователь не найден' });

    await prisma.$transaction([
      prisma.user.update({
        where: { id: userId },
        data: {
          isBlocked: true,
          blockedAt: new Date(),
          blockedBy: req.user.name,
          blockReason: reason
        }
      }),
      prisma.userBlock.create({
        data: {
          userId,
          blockedBy: req.user.name,
          reason
        }
      }),
      prisma.adminAction.create({
        data: {
          adminId: req.user.id,
          actionType: 'BLOCK_USER',
          targetUserId: userId,
          details: reason
        }
      })
    ]);

    res.json({ success: true });
  } catch (e) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
  }
});

app.post('/admin/users/:id/unblock', adminMiddleware, async (req, res) =\u003e {
  try {
    const userId = parseInt(req.params.id);

    const user = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
    if (!user) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Пользователь не найден' });

    const activeBlock = await prisma.userBlock.findFirst({
      where: { userId, unblockedAt: null },
      orderBy: { blockedAt: 'desc' }
    });

    await prisma.$transaction([
      prisma.user.update({
        where: { id: userId },
        data: {
          isBlocked: false,
          blockedAt: null,
          blockedBy: null,
          blockReason: null
        }
      }),
      ...(activeBlock ? [
        prisma.userBlock.update({
          where: { id: activeBlock.id },
          data: { unblockedAt: new Date() }
        })
      ] : []),
      prisma.adminAction.create({
        data: {
          adminId: req.user.id,
          actionType: 'UNBLOCK_USER',
          targetUserId: userId
        }
      })
    ]);

    res.json({ success: true });
  } catch (e) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
  }
});

  Future\u003cvoid\u003e _handleVerifyCode() async {

  Widget _buildQuizQuestionsList() {
    return Column(
      crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.stretch,
      children: [
        Text(

        const SizedBox(height: 24),
        ..._quizQuestions.map((q) {
          final questionText = q['question'];
          final options = q['options'] as List\u003cdynamic\u003e;

          return Card(
            margin: const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: 16),
            color: const Color(0xFF0A0D1A),
            shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16), side: const BorderSide(color: Color(0xFF1E293B))),
            child: Padding(

                    questionText,

                  ),
                  const SizedBox(height: 16),

                    final isSelected = _selectedAnswers[questionText] == opt;
                    return Container(
                      margin: const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: 8),
                      decoration: BoxDecoration(
                        color: isSelected ? const Color(0xFF0066FF).withValues(alpha: 0.15) : Colors.transparent,

                        border: Border.all(color: isSelected ? const Color(0xFF0066FF) : const Color(0xFF1E293B)),
                      ),
                      child: ListTile(
                        dense: true,
                        title: Text(opt.toString(), style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.white)),
                        onTap: () {
                          setState(() {
                            _selectedAnswers[questionText] = opt.toString();

                        },
                      ),
                    );
                  })
                ],
              ),
            ),
          );
        }),
        const SizedBox(height: 24),
        ElevatedButton(
          style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(

                resetBtn = `\u003cbutton class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="resetUserTimer(${udData.user.id}, ${s.id})" style="padding:4px 8px; font-size:0.75rem"\u003eСбросить таймер\u003c/button\u003e`;
              }
            } else if (s.type === 'quiz') {
              const remainingCooldownMinutes = s.cooldownUntil ? Math.ceil((new Date(s.cooldownUntil).getTime() - Date.now()) / 1000 / 60) : 0;
              details = `Попыток: ${s.quizAttempts}/5 ${s.status === 'completed' ? `(Балл: ${s.timeSpentSeconds}%)` : ''}`;
              if (remainingCooldownMinutes \u003e 0) {
                details += ` \u003cbr\u003e\u003cspan style="color:#F59E0B"\u003eКулдаун: ${remainingCooldownMinutes} мин\u003c/span\u003e`;
              }
              if (s.quizAttempts \u003e 0) {
                resetBtn = `\u003cbutton class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="resetUserQuiz(${udData.user.id}, ${s.id})" style="padding:4px 8px; font-size:0.75rem"\u003eСбросить попытки\u003c/button\u003e`;
              }
            }

            const statusColors = {completed: '#10B981', in_progress: '#3B82F6', not_started: 'var(--text-muted)'};
            const statusLabels = {completed: 'Пройден', in_progress: 'В процессе', not_started: 'Не начат'};

            return `
              \u003ctr style="border-bottom:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.03)"\u003e
                \u003ctd style="padding:8px 4px; font-weight:600"\u003e${esc(s.title)} ${s.isFinalExam ? '\u003cspan style="color:#EF4444; font-size:0.7rem; border:1px solid #EF4444; padding:2px 4px; border-radius:4px; margin-left:4px"\u003eЭкзамен\u003c/span\u003e' : ''}\u003c/td\u003e

                \u003ctd style="padding:8px 4px; color:${statusColors[s.status]}"\u003e${statusLabels[s.status]}\u003c/td\u003e

            `;

}

function renderUdTimeline() {
  const container = document.getElementById('ud-timeline-container');
  if (!udData || !udData.timeline.length) {
    container.innerHTML = '\u003cp style="color:var(--text-muted)"\u003eИстория активности пуста\u003c/p\u003e';
    return;
  }

  container.innerHTML = `
    \u003cdiv style="position:relative; padding-left:20px; border-left:2px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.05)"\u003e
      ${udData.timeline.map(t =\u003e {
        let color = '#3B82F6'; // blue
        if (t.type === 'violation') color = '#EF4444'; // red
        if (t.type === 'progress_update' \u0026\u0026 t.message.includes('completed')) color = '#10B981'; // green

        return `
          \u003cdiv style="margin-bottom:16px; position:relative"\u003e
            \u003cspan style="position:absolute; left:-27px; top:4px; width:12px; height:12px; border-radius:50%; background:${color}; border:2px solid var(--bg-card)"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e
            \u003cdiv style="font-size:0.75rem; color:var(--text-muted)"\u003e${new Date(t.timestamp).toLocaleString('ru-RU')}\u003c/div\u003e
            \u003cdiv style="font-size:0.85rem; font-weight:600; color:white; margin-top:2px"\u003e${esc(t.message)}\u003c/div\u003e
          \u003c/div\u003e
        `;
      }).join('')}
    \u003c/div\u003e
  `;
}

async function toggleUserBlock(userId, isBlocked) {
  let reason = '';
  if (!isBlocked) {
    reason = prompt('Укажите причину блокировки пользователя:');
    if (reason === null) return; // cancel
    if (!reason.trim()) reason = 'Нарушение правил платформы';
  } else {
    if (!confirm('Разблокировать доступ пользователю?')) return;
  }

  const endpoint = isBlocked ? `/admin/users/${userId}/unblock` : `/admin/users/${userId}/block`;
  const body = isBlocked ? {} : { reason };

  try {
    await api(endpoint, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify(body)
    });
    
    // Refresh lists
    loadUsersDashboard();
    if (currentDetailUserId === userId) {
      viewUserDetails(userId);
    }
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error toggling block:', err);
  }
}

async function resetUserQuiz(userId, stepId) {
  if (!confirm('Вы уверены, что хотите сбросить попытки прохождения теста и кулдаун?')) return;
  try {
    await api(`/admin/users/${userId}/reset-quiz`, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify({ stepId })
    });
    viewUserDetails(userId);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error resetting quiz:', err);
  }
}

  if (!confirm('Вы уверены, что хотите сбросить таймер урока? Пользователю придется смотреть его заново.')) return;
  try {
    await api(`/admin/users/${userId}/reset-timer`, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify({ stepId })
    });
    viewUserDetails(userId);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Error resetting timer:', err);
  }

### 👤 Ассистент:
Changes Made

### 1. Database \u0026 Migrations
- Modified `backend/prisma/schema.prisma` to add:
  - `UserBlock`: Tracks user blocking history.
  - `AdminAction`: Audit logs for all administrator overrides.
  - `ScreenshotViolation`: Logs each screenshot/recording attempt with step mapping.
  - `UserCourseBlock`: Temporarily locks specific course progress for 24 hours upon 5 violations.
  - `UserLessonProgress`: Added `scrollCompleted`, `timeSpentSeconds`, `lessonStartedAt`, `isTimerCompleted`, `quizAttempts`, and `cooldownUntil`.
- Sync and seeded all courses (21-25) with video URLs, durations, and 5 final exam questions.

### 2. Backend Security \u0026 Progression Gating (`backend/server.js`)
- **Progression Controls:** Enforced step order check (cannot start step `i` unless `i-1` is completed) and final exam check (cannot start unless all module steps are completed).
- **Text Scroll \u0026 Reading Time:** Checks word count to calculate minimal read time (`estimatedReadTime = words / 200 * 60` seconds) and rejects completion if client is faster or scroll is incomplete.
- **Video Countdown Timer:** Records `lessonStartedAt` on the server upon `/start` and rejects `/complete` until duration is fully elapsed.
- **Quiz Shuffling \u0026 Guess Protection:**
  - Shuffles questions and their options on GET, and removes the correct `answer` index from payloads.
  - Compares submitted option text with correct option text securely on the backend.
  - Enforces 80% passing score on quizzes and 95% on final exams.
  - Cooldowns: 30 minutes after 2nd fail, 24 hours after 4th, blocks quiz after 5th.
- **Screenshot Ban:** `/violation` logs screenshot attempts and locks course progress for 24 hours after 5 violations.
- **Certificate Issuance:** Evaluates completion on the backend (90%+ video timers completed, 80%+ intermediate quizzes, 95%+ final exam, 95%+ overall average score), generating a unique UUID.
- **Public Certificate Checker:** A premium-designed public route `GET /verify-certificate/:uuid` with dark styling and metallic gradients verifying graduation details.
- **Admin Endpoints:** Added active user dashboard (search, sort, filter), detail logs, block/unblock reason forms, and overrides (reset attempts/cooldowns, reset video timer).

### 3. Mobile App (Flutter) (`mobile/lib/api_service.dart` \u0026 `mobile/lib/course_detail_screen.dart`)
- **FLAG_SECURE:** Added `flutter_windowmanager` to prevent screenshots/screen recording on Android lessons.
- **Reading Time \u0026 Scroll Tracking:** Linked a ScrollController to verify scrolling, with a countdown bar blocking "Завершить урок" until duration passes.
- **Video Counter:** Displays countdown timer ("Следующий шаг доступен через XX:XX") blocking the button.
- **Violations Simulator:** Added a top bar button `Icons.screenshot_monitor` allowing users to simulate screenshots. Shows warnings at 3 attempts and blocks course for 24h at 5 attempts.
- **Randomized Quizzes:** Dynamic form displaying shuffled questions and options, enforcing cooldown lockouts and listing topics to study upon failure.
- **Dispose Fix:** Wrapped `auth_screen.dart` setState calls with `mounted` checks.

### 4. Admin Dashboard UI (`web/admin/index.html` \u0026 `web/js/admin.js`)
- **Active Users Grid:** Table showing Name, Email, Course, Start Date, Last Activity, Progress %, Status, and Actions, with search inputs and sort options.
- **Detailed Progress Modal:** Tabs containing full step statuses, video timers, quiz attempts, last attempt dates, and a complete chronological activity timeline.
- **Block Toggle:** Quick toggle prompting for block reason and logging history.
- **Override Buttons:** "Сбросить таймер" and "Сбросить попытки" in detailed views to override constraints dynamically.

### Что сейчас происходит с мобильным приложением:

Мобильное приложение находится на **финальной стадии запуска (установка на устройство)**. 

Сборка заняла некоторое время из-за следующих решенных проблем:
1. **Совместимость с Android Gradle Plugin (AGP) 8.0+:** Старый плагин `flutter_windowmanager` не содержал обязательного свойства `namespace` в конфигурации. Мы заменили его на поддерживаемый форк `flutter_windowmanager_plus` и обновили импорты в кодовой базе.
2. **Отсутствие SDK платформ:** На локальном ПК отсутствовали платформы Android SDK 28 и 33. Gradle автоматически принял лицензии, скачал и установил обе платформы перед компиляцией.

Сборка только что завершилась успехом (`

### 👤 Ассистент:

app.post('/admin/create-admin', superAdminMiddleware, async (req, res) =\u003e {
  try {
    const { name, email, password, role } = req.body;
    if (!name || !email || !password) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Имя, email и пароль обязательны' });
    if (!['admin', 'superadmin'].includes(role)) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Недопустимая роль. Допустимые: admin, superadmin' });
    const existing = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { email } });
    if (existing) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Пользователь с таким email уже существует' });
    const hashedPass = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);
    const admin = await prisma.user.create({
      data: { name, email, password: hashedPass, role },
    });
    // Log admin action
    await prisma.adminAction.create({
      data: { adminId: req.user.id, actionType: 'create_admin', targetUserId: admin.id, details: `Создан ${role}: ${email}` }
    });
    res.json({ success: true, user: { id: admin.id, name: admin.name, email: admin.email, role: admin.role } });
  } catch (e) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
  }
});

app.patch('/admin/users/:id/role', superAdminMiddleware, async (req, res) =\u003e {
  try {
    const userId = parseInt(req.params.id);
    const { role } = req.body;
    const allowed = ['user', 'moderator', 'admin', 'superadmin'];
    if (!allowed.includes(role)) return res.status(400).json({ error: `Недопустимая роль. Допустимые: ${allowed.join(', ')}` });
    // Cannot change own role
    if (userId === req.user.id) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Нельзя изменить свою собственную роль' });
    const updated = await prisma.user.update({
      where: { id: userId },
      data: { role },
      select: { id: true, name: true, email: true, role: true }
    });
    await prisma.adminAction.create({
      data: { adminId: req.user.id, actionType: 'change_role', targetUserId: userId, details: `Роль изменена на: ${role}` }
    });
    res.json({ success: true, user: updated });
  } catch (e) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
  }
});

// Order delivery address
app.post('/orders/:id/delivery', authMiddleware, async (req, res) =\u003e {
  try {
    const orderId = parseInt(req.params.id);
    const { deliveryAddress, deliveryCity, deliveryContact } = req.body;
    const order = await prisma.order.findUnique({ where: { id: orderId } });
    if (!order) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Заказ не найден' });
    if (order.userId !== req.user.id) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Нет доступа к этому заказу' });
    // Store delivery info in status field as JSON (minimal schema change)
    const deliveryInfo = JSON.stringify({ deliveryAddress, deliveryCity, deliveryContact });
    const updated = await prisma.order.update({
      where: { id: orderId },
      data: { status: order.status === 'PENDING' ? `PENDING|${deliveryInfo}` : order.status },
    });
    res.json({ success: true, order: updated });
  } catch (e) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });
  }
});

  Widget _buildQuizQuestionsList() {
    return Column(
      crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.stretch,
      children: [
        Text(
          _isFinalExam ? 'Финальный экзамен модуля' : 'Промежуточный тест',
          style: const TextStyle(color: Color(0xFF00E5FF), fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, fontSize: 14),
        ),
        const SizedBox(height: 8),
        Text(
          'Необходимо набрать минимум ${_isFinalExam ? "95%" : "80%"} правильных ответов.',
          style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.grey, fontSize: 13),
        ),
        const SizedBox(height: 24),
        ..._quizQuestions.map((q) {
          final questionText = q['question'];
          final options = q['options'] as List\u003cdynamic\u003e;

          return Card(
            margin: const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: 16),
            color: const Color(0xFF0A0D1A),
            shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16), side: const BorderSide(color: Color(0xFF1E293B))),
            child: Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16.0),
              child: Column(
                crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                children: [
                  Text(
                    questionText,
                    style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 16, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, color: Colors.white),
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(height: 16),
                  ...options.map((opt) {
                    final isSelected = _selectedAnswers[questionText] == opt;
                    return Container(
                      margin: const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: 8),
                      decoration: BoxDecoration(
                        color: isSelected ? const Color(0xFF0066FF).withValues(alpha: 0.15) : Colors.transparent,
                        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
                        border: Border.all(color: isSelected ? const Color(0xFF0066FF) : const Color(0xFF1E293B)),
                      ),
                      child: ListTile(
                        dense: true,
                        title: Text(opt.toString(), style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.white)),
                        onTap: () {
                          setState(() {
                            _selectedAnswers[questionText] = opt.toString();
                          });
                        },
                      ),
                    );
                  })
                ],
              ),
            ),
          );
        }),
        const SizedBox(height: 24),
        ElevatedButton(
          style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
            backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF0066FF),
            padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 16),
            shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12)),
          ),
          onPressed: _selectedAnswers.length \u003c _quizQuestions.length ? null : _submitQuizAnswers,
          child: const Text('Сдать тест', style: TextStyle(fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, color: Colors.white, fontSize: 16)),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildQuizResults() {
    final remainingCooldownMinutes = _cooldownUntil != null ? _cooldownUntil!.difference(DateTime.now()).inMinutes : 0;

    return Padding(

            textAlign: TextAlign.center,
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 24),
          Card(
            color: const Color(0xFF0A0D1A),
            shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16)),
            child: Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20.0),
              child: Column(
                children: [
                  _buildResultRow('Ваш результат:', '${_quizScore.toStringAsFixed(0)}%'),
                  const Divider(color: Colors.grey),
                  _buildResultRow('Использовано попыток:', '$_attemptsUsed из 5'),
                  if (!_quizPassed \u0026\u0026 _cooldownUntil != null \u0026\u0026 remainingCooldownMinutes \u003e 0) ...[
                    const Divider(color: Colors.grey),
                    _buildResultRow('Повтор доступен через:', '$remainingCooldownMinutes мин'),
                  ]
                ],
              ),
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 24),
          if (!_quizPassed \u0026\u0026 _failedTopics.isNotEmpty) ...[
            const Text(
              'Темы, которые нужно повторить:',
              style: TextStyle(fontSize: 16, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, color: Colors.white),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 8),
            ..._failedTopics.map((topic) =\u003e Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 4.0),

              style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
                backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF1E293B),
                padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 16),
              ),
              onPressed: remainingCooldownMinutes \u003e 0 || _attemptsUsed \u003e= 5
                  ? null
                  : () {
                      setState(() {
                        _quizSubmitted = false;
                        _selectedAnswers.clear();
                      });
                    },
              child: Text(
                _attemptsUsed \u003e= 5
                    ? 'Попытки исчерпаны (обратитесь к админу)'

                style: const TextStyle(fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, color: Colors.white),
              ),
            ),
          const SizedBox(height: 12),
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () =\u003e Navigator.of(context).pop(),
            child: const Text('Вернуться к списку уроков'),
          )
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildResultRow(String title, String value) {

          Text(value, style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.white, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, fontSize: 15)),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

l{"CodeContent":"import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class HomeScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const HomeScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State\u003cHomeScreen\u003e createState() =\u003e _HomeScreenState();
}

class _HomeScreenState extends State\u003cHomeScreen\u003e {
  late Future\u003cList\u003cdynamic\u003e\u003e _coursesFuture;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _coursesFuture = ApiService.fetchCourses();
  }

  void _refreshCourses() {
    setState(() {
      _coursesFuture = ApiService.fetchCourses();
    });
  }

  /// Find the current active course (in_progress or last started)
  Map\u003cString, dynamic\u003e? _findActiveCourse(List\u003cdynamic\u003e courses) {
    // First: find a course with in_progress steps
    for (final c in courses) {
      if (c['isLocked'] == true) continue;
      final steps = c['steps'] as List\u003cdynamic\u003e? ?? [];
      final hasInProgress = steps.any((s) =\u003e s['userProgress']?['status'] == 'in_progress');
      final hasCompleted = steps.any((s) =\u003e s['userProgress']?['status'] == 'completed');
      if (hasInProgress || hasCompleted) return c as Map\u003cString, dynamic\u003e;
    }
    // Fallback: first unlocked course
    for (final c in courses) {
      if (c['isLocked'] != true) return c as Map\u003cString, dynamic\u003e;
    }
    return null;
  }

  /// True if user has any progress in a course
  bool _hasProgress(Map\u003cString, dynamic\u003e course) {
    final steps = course['steps'] as List\u003cdynamic\u003e? ?? [];
    return steps.any((s) {
      final status = s['userProgress']?['status'];
      return status == 'in_progress' || status == 'completed';
    });
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return ValueListenableBuilder\u003cString\u003e(
      valueListenable: AppState().currentLanguage,
      builder: (context, lang, child) {
        final state = AppState();
        final isDark = Theme.of(context).brightness == Brightness.dark;

          appBar: AppBar(
            title: Text(
              state.translate('courses_title'),
              style: const TextStyle(fontWeight: FontWeight.w900),
            ),
            backgroundColor: Colors.transparent,
            elevation: 0,
            actions: [
              IconButton(
                icon: const Icon(Icons.refresh),
                onPressed: _refreshCourses,
              )

          ),

            onRefresh: () async =\u003e _refreshCourses(),
            child: FutureBuilder\u003cList\u003cdynamic\u003e\u003e(
              future: _coursesFuture,
              builder: (context, snapshot) {
                if (snapshot.connectionState == ConnectionState.waiting) {
                  return const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator());
                }
                if (snapshot.hasError || !snapshot.hasData || snapshot.data!.isEmpty) {
                  return ListView(
                    padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
                    children: [
                      _buildPromoBanner(state, null, isDark),
                      const SizedBox(height: 32),
                      Text(
                        state.translate('courses_all'),
                        style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 20, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold),

                      const Center(
                        child: Text(

                          style: TextStyle(color: Colors.grey),
                        ),
                      ),
                    ],
                  );
                }

                final courses = snapshot.data!;
                final activeCourse = _findActiveCourse(courses);
                final bannerCourse = activeCourse ?? (courses.isNotEmpty ? courses.first as Map\u003cString, dynamic\u003e : null);

                return ListView.builder(
                  padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
                  itemCount: courses.length + 2, // 1 banner + 1 title + courses list
                  itemBuilder: (context, index) {
                    if (index == 0) {
                      return _buildPromoBanner(state, bannerCourse, isDark, activeCourse: activeCourse, courses: courses);

  List\u003cLatLng\u003e _parseCoordinates(dynamic raw) {
    List\u003cLatLng\u003e points = [];
    if (raw == null) return points;

    if (raw is List \u0026\u0026 raw.isNotEmpty \u0026\u0026 raw.first is List \u0026\u0026 raw.first.first is List) {
      raw = raw.first;
    }

    if (raw is List) {
      for (var item in raw) {
        if (item is List \u0026\u0026 item.length \u003e= 2) {
          try {
            double lng = double.parse(item[0].toString());
            double lat = double.parse(item[1].toString());
            points.add(LatLng(lat, lng));
          } catch (_) {}
        }
      }
    }
    return points;
  }

  double _getBoundsArea(List\u003cLatLng\u003e points) {
    if (points.isEmpty) return 0.0;
    double minLat = 90.0, maxLat = -90.0, minLng = 180.0, maxLng = -180.0;
    for (var p in points) {
      if (p.latitude \u003c minLat) minLat = p.latitude;
      if (p.latitude \u003e maxLat) maxLat = p.latitude;
      if (p.longitude \u003c minLng) minLng = p.longitude;
      if (p.longitude \u003e maxLng) maxLng = p.longitude;
    }
    return (maxLat - minLat) * (maxLng - minLng);
  }

  void _showZoneDetails(String name, String type, String maxAltitude) {

### 👤 Ассистент:
**Analyzing Admin Access**

I've been examining the `web/js/admin.js` file, specifically lines 11-33. The script checks for a token and an admin role before displaying the admin app. Otherwise, it presents a login form. It seems access control hinges on these two factors. I am now exploring how the token and admin role are initially established.


**Identifying Access Vulnerability**

I've discovered a critical access vulnerability! The client-side code in `admin.js` specifically checks for `role === 'admin'` during login. However, the seeded admin user's role is set to `'superadmin'` in `seed.js`. This mismatch causes the login process to fail, displaying the "Нет доступа администратора" (No admin access) error. This is because the code does not consider the `superadmin` role to be an admin role. I suspect this will cause significant issues when trying to log in as a superadmin.

### 2. Запуск проекта и исправление ошибки доступа администратора
Проект успешно запущен, и все ошибки исправлены:

1. **База данных настроена и заполнена:**
   * Схема данных синхронизирована с PostgreSQL с помощью `prisma db push`.
   * База данных наполнена всеми необходимыми начальными данными: создан суперадминистратор, добавлены интерактивные зоны воздушного пространства, курсы и информационные разделы.

2. **Backend-сервер запущен:**
   * Проект запущен на порту **3000** и работает в фоновом режиме:
     * **Публичный сайт:** [http://localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000)
     * **Админ-панель:** [http://localhost:3000/admin](http://localhost:3000/admin)

3. **Исправлена ошибка доступа (`Нет доступа администратора`):**
   * **Причина:** Пользователь `admin@skycheck.uz` создается в базе данных с ролью `superadmin`. Однако во фронтенде ([admin.js](file:///d:/skycheck/web/js/admin.js)) стояла жесткая проверка, которая пропускала только пользователей с ролью `admin` и блокировала `superadmin`.
   * **Решение:** Мы обновили логику авторизации во фронтенде в [admin.js](file:///d:/skycheck/web/js/admin.js), разрешив вход как для `admin`, так и для `superadmin`.

> [!IMPORTANT]
> **Для входа в панель администратора:**
> 1. Откройте [http://localhost:3000/admin](http://localhost:3000/admin).
> 2. **Обязательно сделайте жесткую перезагрузку страницы (Ctrl + F5)**, чтобы ваш браузер сбросил старый кэш и загрузил обновленный файл `admin.js`.
> 3. Войдите, используя данные:
>    * **Email:** `admin@skycheck.uz`
>    * **Пароль:** `admin123`Z

Вчерашний чат не отображается в текущем окне по следующим техническим причинам:

Чтобы старые обсуждения не перегружали память модели (контекст) и не замедляли ответы, среда разработки по умолчанию открывает **новую чистую сессию** при перезапуске или начале нового рабочего дня.

### 👤 Ассистент:
расширена переменными: `scrollCompleted` (прокрутка выполнена), `timeSpentSeconds` (проведенное время), `lessonStartedAt` (время начала), `isTimerCompleted` (таймер завершен), `quizAttempts` (число попыток теста), `cooldownUntil` (время окончания штрафного кулдауна).
* База данных наполнена курсами и вопросами к финальным экзаменам.

### 2. Безопасность и логика бэкенда (`server.js`)
* **Контроль последовательности:** Добавлены серверные проверки, запрещающие проходить шаг `i`, если не завершен шаг `i-1`, и запрещающие доступ к экзамену модуля, пока не прочитаны все его лекции.
* **Проверка времени чтения текста:** Сервер высчитывает минимальное время на прочтение статьи по формуле: `кол-во слов / 200 * 60` секунд. Если запрос на завершение отправлен слишком быстро, сервер возвращает ошибку.
* **Таймер видео:** Время начала фиксируется на сервере, завершить видео-урок раньше длительности ролика невозможно.
* **Защита тестов от угадывания:**
  * Вопросы и варианты ответов перемешиваются на бэкенде при каждом запросе.
  * Правильный индекс ответа удаляется из JSON, отправляемого клиенту. Проверка выбранного ответа происходит по сравнению текста.
  * Введены лимиты: кулдаун 30 минут после 2-го провала теста, 24 часа после 4-го, и полная блокировка теста после 5 неудачных попыток.
* **Блокировка за скриншоты:** При вызове `/violation` фиксируется нарушение. На 5-е нарушение курс блокируется на сутки.
* **Генерация сертификатов:** При просмотре более 90% видео, сдаче всех тестов на 80%+ и экзамена на 95%+ с общим средним баллом от 95% генерируется официальный сертификат с уникальным UUID.
* **Веб-проверка сертификатов:** Создан красивый публичный веб-интерфейс проверки сертификатов по адресу `/verify-certificate/:uuid`.

### 3. Мобильное приложение (Flutter)
* **Защита контента:** Подключена библиотека `flutter_windowmanager` (блокирует скриншоты и запись экрана на Android во время уроков).
* **Симулятор нарушений:** Добавлена кнопка имитации скриншота (иконка монитора сверху). Показывает предупреждения на 3-й попытке и блокирует курс на 24 часа на 5-й.
* **Отображение тестов:** Динамическая форма выводит перемешанные вопросы и варианты, а при провале теста показывает список тем, которые нужно подучить.

### 4. Интерфейс панели администратора
* **Список активных учеников:** Таблица отображает ФИО, Email, Курс, Дату старта, Последнюю активность, % Прогресса, Статус блокировки.
* **Модальное окно прогресса:** Показывает детальный статус по каждому уроку, завершенность таймеров, количество попыток теста, оставшееся время кулдауна и полную ленту активности ученика.
* **Админ-переопределения:** Кнопки
